liability matching asset diversification and hedging the fixed income target asset allocation match the bond like and long dated nature of the pension obligation asset are broadly diversified within asset class to achieve risk adjusted return that in total lower asset volatility relative to the obligation strategy to address the goal of ensuring sufficient asset to pay benefit include target allocation to broad array of asset class and strategy within asset class that provide adequate return diversification and liquidity motor company and subsidiariesnotes to the financial statementsnote retirement benefit continued derivative are permitted for fixed income investment and public equity manager to use efficient substitute for traditional security and to manage exposure to interest rate and foreign exchange risk interest rate and foreign currency derivative instrument are used for the purpose of hedging change in the fair value of asset that result from interest rate change and currency fluctuation interest rate derivative also are used to adjust portfolio duration derivative may not be used to leverage or to alter the economic exposure to an asset class outside the scope of the mandate an investment manager ha been given alternative investment manager are permitted to employ leverage including through the use of derivative or other tool that may alter economic exposure alternative investment execute diverse strategy that provide exposure to broad range of hedge fund strategy equity investment in private company and investment in private property fund significant concentration of risk significant concentration of risk in our plan asset relate to interest rate growth asset and operating risk in order to minimize asset volatility relative to the obligation the majority of plan asset are allocated to fixed income investment which are exposed to interest rate risk rate increase generally will result in decline in the value of fixed income asset while reducing the present value of the obligation conversely rate decrease generally will increase the value of fixed income asset offsetting the related increase in the obligation in order to ensure asset are sufficient to pay benefit portion of plan asset is allocated to growth asset that are expected over time to earn higher return with more volatility than fixed income investment which more closely match pension obligation within growth asset risk is mitigated by constructing portfolio that is broadly diversified by asset class investment strategy manager style and process operating risk include the risk of inadequate diversification and weak control to mitigate these risk investment are diversified across and within asset class in support of investment objective policy and practice to address operating risk include ongoing manager oversight style adherence team strength firm health and internal risk control plan and asset class investment guideline and instruction that are communicated to manager and periodic compliance review to ensure adherence at year end ford security comprised le than of our plan asset expected long term rate of return on asset the long term return an entity that either ha insufficient equity to finance it activity without additional subordinated financial support or ii ha equity investor who lack the characteristic of controlling financial interest we consolidate vies of which we are the primary beneficiary we consider the primary beneficiary of vie when we have both the power to direct the activity that most significantly impact the entity economic performance and the obligation to absorb loss or the right to receive benefit from the entity that could potentially be significant to the vie asset recognized result of consolidating these vies do not represent additional asset that could be used to satisfy claim against our general asset liability recognized result of consolidating these vies do not represent additional claim on our general asset rather they represent claim against the specific asset of the consolidated vies we have the power to direct the significant activity of an entity when our management ha the ability to make key operating decision such decision regarding capital investment or manufacturing production schedule for securitization entity we have the power to direct significant activity when we have the ability to exercise discretion in the servicing of financial asset issue additional debt exercise unilateral call option add asset to revolving structure or control investment decision vies of which we are not the primary beneficiarycertain of our investment in affiliate are vies in which the power to direct economically significant activity is shared with other investor our investment in similar nature the specific fact and circumstance asserted the likelihood that we will prevail and the severity of any potential loss we reevaluate and update our accrual matter progress over time for the majority of matter which generally arise out of alleged defect in our product we establish an accrual based on our extensive historical experience with similar matter we do not believe there is reasonably possible outcome materially in excess of our accrual for these matter for the remaining matter where our historical experience with similar matter is of more limited value non pattern matter we evaluate the matter primarily based on the individual fact and circumstance for non pattern matter we evaluate whether there is reasonable possibility of material loss in excess of any
